        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

        }

        }

          flex-grow: 0;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

CRASH ANALYSIS



<span class="line"><!---->CRASH ANALYSIS<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. When v8 intends to share an EXTRA-LONG string, the string object may no longer be kept in the shared memory, thus triggering the DCHECK [1].



<span class="line"><!---->1. When v8 intends to share an EXTRA-LONG string, the string object may no longer be kept in the shared memory, thus triggering the DCHECK [1].<!----></span>



<br>





2. After DCHECK, there is an operation related to the write barrier [2], and since the string object is no longer on shared memory, this operation may change the stability of current memory region, causing a potential UAF vulnerabilit.



<span class="line"><!---->2. After DCHECK, there is an operation related to the write barrier [2], and since the string object is no longer on shared memory, this operation may change the stability of current memory region, causing a potential UAF vulnerabilit.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





Handle<String> String::Share(Isolate* isolate, Handle<String> string) {



<span class="line"><!---->Handle&lt;String&gt; String::Share(Isolate* isolate, Handle&lt;String&gt; string) {<!----></span>



<br>





  DCHECK(v8_flags.shared_string_table);



<span class="line"><!---->  DCHECK(v8_flags.shared_string_table);<!----></span>



<br>





  MaybeHandle<Map> new_map;



<span class="line"><!---->  MaybeHandle&lt;Map&gt; new_map;<!----></span>



<br>





  switch (



<span class="line"><!---->  switch (<!----></span>



<br>





      isolate->factory()->ComputeSharingStrategyForString(string, &new_map)) {



<span class="line"><!---->      isolate-&gt;factory()-&gt;ComputeSharingStrategyForString(string, &amp;new_map)) {<!----></span>



<br>





    case StringTransitionStrategy::kCopy:



<span class="line"><!---->    case StringTransitionStrategy::kCopy:<!----></span>



<br>





      return SlowShare(isolate, string);



<span class="line"><!---->      return SlowShare(isolate, string);<!----></span>



<br>





    case StringTransitionStrategy::kInPlace:



<span class="line"><!---->    case StringTransitionStrategy::kInPlace:<!----></span>



<br>





      // A relaxed write is sufficient here, because at this point the string



<span class="line"><!---->      // A relaxed write is sufficient here, because at this point the string<!----></span>



<br>





      // has not yet escaped the current thread.



<span class="line"><!---->      // has not yet escaped the current thread.<!----></span>



<br>





      DCHECK(string->InSharedHeap());    <------------------------------------- [1]



<span class="line"><!---->      DCHECK(string-&gt;InSharedHeap());    &lt;------------------------------------- [1]<!----></span>



<br>





      string->set_map_no_write_barrier(*new_map.ToHandleChecked()); <---------- [2]



<span class="line"><!---->      string-&gt;set_map_no_write_barrier(*new_map.ToHandleChecked()); &lt;---------- [2]<!----></span>



<br>





      return string;



<span class="line"><!---->      return string;<!----></span>



<br>





    case StringTransitionStrategy::kAlreadyTransitioned:



<span class="line"><!---->    case StringTransitionStrategy::kAlreadyTransitioned:<!----></span>



<br>





      return string;



<span class="line"><!---->      return string;<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>

[heap] Also promote strings in large objects into shared heap



<span class="line"><!---->[heap] Also promote strings in large objects into shared heap<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





With --shared-string-table all in-place internalizable strings are



<span class="line"><!---->With --shared-string-table all in-place internalizable strings are<!----></span>



<br>





directly promoted from new space into the shared heap. However, this



<span class="line"><!---->directly promoted from new space into the shared heap. However, this<!----></span>



<br>





wasn't the case with large objects. This CL fixes this and adds test



<span class="line"><!---->wasn't the case with large objects. This CL fixes this and adds test<!----></span>



<br>





to guide fuzzers.



<span class="line"><!---->to guide fuzzers.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/v8/issues/detail?id=13267" title="Implement shared space isolate for shared heap"><!---->Bug: v8:13267<!----></a>

[string] Copy when sharing strings that are not in shared space



<span class="line"><!---->[string] Copy when sharing strings that are not in shared space<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Usually sharable strings are automatically promoted to shared old space



<span class="line"><!---->Usually sharable strings are automatically promoted to shared old space<!----></span>



<br>





and can be shared in-place.



<span class="line"><!---->and can be shared in-place.<!----></span>



<br>





There are currently two exceptions:



<span class="line"><!---->There are currently two exceptions:<!----></span>



<br>





- When using a non-moving GC (e.g. minor MC)



<span class="line"><!---->- When using a non-moving GC (e.g. minor MC)<!----></span>



<br>





- Strings in LO space



<span class="line"><!---->- Strings in LO space<!----></span>



<br>





Account for these exceptions by copying strings to the respective shared



<span class="line"><!---->Account for these exceptions by copying strings to the respective shared<!----></span>



<br>





space when sharing them.



<span class="line"><!---->space when sharing them.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1400048" title="Security:  Debug check failed: string->InSharedHeap() in v8"><!---->Bug: chromium:1400048<!----></a>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
